{
    if (s.length() < 24) throw new ParseException("Invalid ISO8601 format", 0);

    String year = s.substring(0, 4);
    String month = s.substring(5, 7);
    String day = s.substring(8, 10);
    String hour = s.substring(11, 13);
    String minute = s.substring(14, 16);
    String second = s.substring(17, 19);
    String timezone = s.substring(20, 24);

    int yearInt = Integer.parseInt(year);
    int monthInt = Integer.parseInt(month);
    int dayInt = Integer.parseInt(day);
    int hourInt = Integer.parseInt(hour);
    int minuteInt = Integer.parseInt(minute);
    int secondInt = Integer.parseInt(second);
    int timezoneOffset = Integer.parseInt(timezone);

    Calendar calendar = Calendar.getInstance();
    calendar.set(yearInt, monthInt - 1, dayInt, hourInt, minuteInt, secondInt);
    calendar.setTimeZone(TimeZone.getTimeZone("GMT" + (timezoneOffset >= 0 ? "+" : "") + String.format("%02d", timezoneOffset)));

    return calendar.getTime();
}

### Implementation 1

```java
{
    String s = in.nextString();
    // Needs to be synchronized since JDK DateFormat classes are not thread-safe
    synchronized (dateFormats) {
        for (DateFormat dateFormat : dateFormats) {
            TimeZone originalTimeZone = dateFormat.getTimeZone();
            try {
                dateFormat.setTimeZone(TimeZone.getDefault());
                Date date = dateFormat.parse(s);
                dateFormat.setTimeZone(originalTimeZone);
                return date;
            } catch (ParseException e) {
                // Ignore and continue with the next format
            }
        }
    }

    throw new JsonSyntaxException("Failed parsing '" + s + "' as Date; at path " + in.getPreviousPath());
}
```

### Implementation 2

```java
{
    String s = in.nextString();
    // Needs to be synchronized since JDK DateFormat classes are not thread-safe
    synchronized (dateFormats) {
        for (DateFormat dateFormat : dateFormats) {
            TimeZone originalTimeZone = dateFormat.getTimeZone();
            try {
                dateFormat.setTimeZone(TimeZone.getDefault());
                return dateFormat.parse(s);
            } catch (ParseException e) {
                // Ignore and continue with the next format
            } finally {
                dateFormat.setTimeZone(originalTimeZone);
            }
        }
    }

    throw new JsonSyntaxException("Failed parsing '" + s + "' as Date; at path " + in.getPreviousPath());
}
```

### Explanation:
1. **Implementation 1**:
   - The `parse` method is called inside the try block.
   - If a `ParseException` occurs, it is caught and ignored, allowing the loop to continue with the next format.
   - After attempting to parse, regardless of success or failure, the original time zone is restored.

2. **Implementation 2**:
   - The `parse` method is called inside the try block.
   - If a `ParseException` occurs, it is caught and ignored, allowing the loop to continue with the next format.
   - The original time zone is always restored in the finally block, ensuring that the time zone is reset even if an exception occurs.

Both implementations ensure that the `DateFormat` objects are not modified outside of their synchronized block, maintaining thread safety.

    synchronized (dateFormats) {
        for (DateFormat dateFormat : dateFormats) {
            TimeZone originalTimeZone = dateFormat.getTimeZone();
            try {
                return dateFormat.parse(s);
            } catch (ParseException ignored) {
                // OK: try the next format
            } finally {
                dateFormat.setTimeZone(originalTimeZone);
            }
        }
    }
    try {
        return ISO8601Utils.parse(s, new ParsePosition(0));
    } catch (ParseException e) {
        throw new JsonSyntaxException("Failed parsing '" + s + "' as Date; at path " + in.getPreviousPath(), e);
    }
}

2026-04-03 12:58:13 gin.test.ExternalTestRunner.createTempDirectory() INFO: Created temp dir: /var/folders/hh/tn08kl1j0xnd2fmc74qdhlz40000gn/T/9527398294649539015
2026-04-03 12:58:13 gin.edit.llm.LLMReplaceStatement.applyMultiple() INFO: Seeking replacements for:
2026-04-03 12:58:13 gin.edit.llm.LLMReplaceStatement.applyMultiple() INFO: {
    Exception fail = null;
    try {
        int offset = pos.getIndex();
        // extract year
        int year = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 4);
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, '-')) {
            offset += 1;
        }
        // extract month
        int month = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, '-')) {
            offset += 1;
        }
        // extract day
        int day = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
        // default time value
        int hour = 0;
        int minutes = 0;
        int seconds = 0;
        // always use 0 otherwise returned date will include millis of current time
        int milliseconds = 0;
        // if the value has no time component (and no time zone), we are done
        boolean hasT = checkOffset(date, offset, 'T');
        if (!hasT && (date.length() <= offset)) {
            Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(year, month - 1, day);
            calendar.setLenient(false);
            pos.setIndex(offset);
            return calendar.getTime();
        }
        if (hasT) {
            // extract hours, minutes, seconds and milliseconds
            hour = parseInt(date, offset += 1, offset += 2);
            if (checkOffset(date, offset, ':')) {
                offset += 1;
            }
            minutes = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
            if (checkOffset(date, offset, ':')) {
                offset += 1;
            }
            // second and milliseconds can be optional
            if (date.length() > offset) {
                char c = date.charAt(offset);
                if (c != 'Z' && c != '+' && c != '-') {
                    seconds = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
                    if (seconds > 59 && seconds < 63) {
                        // truncate up to 3 leap seconds
                        seconds = 59;
                    }
                    // milliseconds can be optional in the format
                    if (checkOffset(date, offset, '.')) {
                        offset += 1;
                        // assume at least one digit
                        int endOffset = indexOfNonDigit(date, offset + 1);
                        // parse up to 3 digits
                        int parseEndOffset = Math.min(endOffset, offset + 3);
                        int fraction = parseInt(date, offset, parseEndOffset);
                        // compensate for "missing" digits
                        switch(// number of digits parsed
                        parseEndOffset - offset) {
                            case 2:
                                milliseconds = fraction * 10;
                                break;
                            case 1:
                                milliseconds = fraction * 100;
                                break;
                            default:
                                milliseconds = fraction;
                        }
                        offset = endOffset;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        // extract timezone
        if (date.length() <= offset) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("No time zone indicator");
        }
        TimeZone timezone = null;
        char timezoneIndicator = date.charAt(offset);
        if (timezoneIndicator == 'Z') {
            timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
            offset += 1;
        } else if (timezoneIndicator == '+' || timezoneIndicator == '-') {
            String timezoneOffset = date.substring(offset);
            // When timezone has no minutes, we should append it, valid timezones are, for example:
            // +00:00, +0000 and +00
            timezoneOffset = timezoneOffset.length() >= 5 ? timezoneOffset : timezoneOffset + "00";
            offset += timezoneOffset.length();
            // 18-Jun-2015, tatu: Minor simplification, skip offset of "+0000"/"+00:00"
            if (timezoneOffset.equals("+0000") || timezoneOffset.equals("+00:00")) {
                timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
            } else {
                // 18-Jun-2015, tatu: Looks like offsets only work from GMT, not UTC...
                // not sure why, but that's the way it looks. Further, Javadocs for
                // `java.util.TimeZone` specifically instruct use of GMT as base for
                // custom timezones... odd.
                String timezoneId = "GMT" + timezoneOffset;
                // String timezoneId = "UTC" + timezoneOffset;
                timezone = TimeZone.getTimeZone(timezoneId);
                String act = timezone.getID();
                if (!act.equals(timezoneId)) {
                    /* 22-Jan-2015, tatu: Looks like canonical version has colons, but we may be given
             *    one without. If so, don't sweat.
             *   Yes, very inefficient. Hopefully not hit often.
             *   If it becomes a perf problem, add 'loose' comparison instead.
             */
                    String cleaned = act.replace(":", "");
                    if (!cleaned.equals(timezoneId)) {
                        throw new IndexOutOfBoundsException("Mismatching time zone indicator: " + timezoneId + " given, resolves to " + timezone.getID());
                    }
                }
            }
        } else {
            throw new IndexOutOfBoundsException("Invalid time zone indicator '" + timezoneIndicator + "'");
        }
        Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(timezone);
        calendar.setLenient(false);
        calendar.set(Calendar.YEAR, year);
        calendar.set(Calendar.MONTH, month - 1);
        calendar.set(Calendar.DAY_OF_MONTH, day);
        calendar.set(Calendar.HOUR_OF_DAY, hour);
        calendar.set(Calendar.MINUTE, minutes);
        calendar.set(Calendar.SECOND, seconds);
        calendar.set(Calendar.MILLISECOND, milliseconds);
        pos.setIndex(offset);
        return calendar.getTime();
        // If we get a ParseException it'll already have the right message/offset.
        // Other exception types can convert here.
    } catch (IndexOutOfBoundsException | IllegalArgumentException e) {
        fail = e;
    }
    String input = (date == null) ? null : ('"' + date + '"');
    String msg = fail.getMessage();
    if (msg == null || msg.isEmpty()) {
        msg = "(" + fail.getClass().getName() + ")";
    }
    ParseException ex = new ParseException("Failed to parse date [" + input + "]: " + msg, pos.getIndex());
    ex.initCause(fail);
    throw ex;
}

    int month = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
    if (checkOffset(date, offset, '-')) {
        offset += 1;
    }
    // extract day
    int day = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
    // default time value
    int hour = 0;
    int minutes = 0;
    int seconds = 0;
    int milliseconds = 0;
    boolean hasT = checkOffset(date, offset, 'T');
    if (!hasT && (date.length() <= offset)) {
        Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(year, month - 1, day);
        calendar.setLenient(false);
        pos.setIndex(offset);
        return calendar.getTime();
    }
    if (hasT) {
        hour = parseInt(date, offset += 1, offset += 2);
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, ':')) {
            offset += 1;
        }
        minutes = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, ':')) {
            offset += 1;
        }
        if (date.length() > offset) {
            char c = date.charAt(offset);
            if (c != 'Z' && c != '+' && c != '-') {
                seconds = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
                if (seconds > 59 && seconds < 63) {
                    seconds = 59;
                }
                if (checkOffset(date, offset, '.')) {
                    offset += 1;
                    int endOffset = indexOfNonDigit(date, offset + 1);
                    int parseEndOffset = Math.min(endOffset, offset + 3);
                    int fraction = parseInt(date, offset, parseEndOffset);
                    switch(parseEndOffset - offset) {
                        case 2:
                            milliseconds = fraction * 10;
                            break;
                        case 1:
                            milliseconds = fraction * 100;
                            break;
                        default:
                            milliseconds = fraction;
                    }
                    offset = endOffset;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    if (date.length() <= offset) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("No time zone indicator");
    }
    TimeZone timezone = null;
    char timezoneIndicator = date.charAt(offset);
    if (timezoneIndicator == 'Z') {
        timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
        offset += 1;
    } else if (timezoneIndicator == '+' || timezoneIndicator == '-') {
        String timezoneOffset = date.substring(offset);
        timezoneOffset = timezoneOffset.length() >= 5 ? timezoneOffset : timezoneOffset + "00";
        offset += timezoneOffset.length();
        if (timezoneOffset.equals("+0000") || timezoneOffset.equals("+00:00")) {
            timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
        } else {
            String timezoneId = "GMT" + timezoneOffset;
            timezone = TimeZone.getTimeZone(timezoneId);
            String act = timezone.getID();
            if (!act.equals(timezoneId)) {
                String cleaned = act.replace(":", "");
                if (!cleaned.equals(timezoneId)) {
                    throw new IndexOutOfBoundsException("Mismatching time zone indicator: " + timezoneId + " given, resolves to " + timezone.getID());
                }
            }
        }
    } else {
        throw new IndexOutOfBoundsException("Invalid time zone indicator '" + timezoneIndicator + "'");
    }
    Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(timezone);
    calendar.setLenient(false);
    calendar.set(Calendar.YEAR, year);
    calendar.set(Calendar.MONTH, month - 1);
    calendar.set(Calendar.DAY_OF_MONTH, day);
    calendar.set(Calendar.HOUR_OF_DAY, hour);
    calendar.set(Calendar.MINUTE, minutes);
    calendar.set(Calendar.SECOND, seconds);
    calendar.set(Calendar.MILLISECOND, milliseconds);
    pos.setIndex(offset);
    return calendar.getTime();
}

        String cleaned = act.replace(":", "");
        if (!cleaned.equals(timezoneId)) {
            throw new IndexOutOfBoundsException("Mismatching time zone indicator: " + timezoneId + " given, resolves to " + timezone.getID());
        }
    }
}

    // 18-Jun-2015, tatu: Looks like offsets only work from GMT, not UTC...
    // not sure why, but that's the way it looks. Further, Javadocs for
    // `java.util.TimeZone` specifically instruct use of GMT as base for
    // custom timezones... odd.
    String timezoneId = "GMT" + timezoneOffset;
    // <<PLACEHOLDER>>
    ;
    // String timezoneId = "UTC" + timezoneOffset;
    String act = timezone.getID();
    if (!act.equals(timezoneId)) {
        /* 22-Jan-2015, tatu: Looks like canonical version has colons, but we may be given
             *    one without. If so, don't sweat.
             *   Yes, very inefficient. Hopefully not hit often.
             *   If it becomes a perf problem, add 'loose' comparison instead.
             */
        String cleaned = act.replace(":", "");
        if (!cleaned.equals(timezoneId)) {
            throw new IndexOutOfBoundsException("Mismatching time zone indicator: " + timezoneId + " given, resolves to " + timezone.getID());
        }
    }
}

2026-04-03 13:00:30 gin.edit.llm.LLMMaskedStatement.maskCode() INFO: {
    seconds = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
    if (seconds > 59 && seconds < 63) {
        // truncate up to 3 leap seconds
        seconds = 59;
    }
    // milliseconds can be optional in the format
    if (checkOffset(date, offset, '.')) {
        offset += 1;
        // assume at least one digit
        int endOffset = indexOfNonDigit(date, offset + 1);
        // <<PLACEHOLDER>>
        ;
        int fraction = parseInt(date, offset, parseEndOffset);
        // compensate for "missing" digits
        switch(// number of digits parsed
        parseEndOffset - offset) {
            case 2:
                milliseconds = fraction * 10;
                break;
            case 1:
                milliseconds = fraction * 100;
                break;
            default:
                milliseconds = fraction;
        }
        offset = endOffset;
    }
}

    seconds = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);

        // truncate up to 3 leap seconds

        switch(// number of digits parsed
        parseEndOffset - offset) {
            case 2:
                milliseconds = fraction * 10;
                break;
            case 1:
                milliseconds = fraction * 100;
                break;
            default:
                milliseconds = fraction;
        }
        offset = endOffset;
    }

    char c = date.charAt(offset);
    if (c != 'Z' && c != '+' && c != '-') {
        seconds = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
        if (seconds > 59 && seconds < 63) {
            // truncate up to 3 leap seconds
            seconds = 59;
        }
        // milliseconds can be optional in the format
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, '.')) {
            offset += 1;
            // assume at least one digit
            int endOffset = indexOfNonDigit(date, offset + 1);
            // parse up to 3 digits
            int parseEndOffset = Math.min(endOffset, offset + 3);
            int fraction = parseInt(date, offset, parseEndOffset);
            // compensate for "missing" digits
            switch(// number of digits parsed
            parseEndOffset - offset) {
                case 2:
                    milliseconds = fraction * 10;
                    break;
                case 1:
                    milliseconds = fraction * 100;
                    break;
                default:
                    milliseconds = fraction;
            }
            offset = endOffset;
        }
    }
}

            seconds = 59;

        // milliseconds can be optional in the format

            offset += 1;
            // assume at least one digit
            int endOffset = indexOfNonDigit(date, offset + 1);

                    break;

                    milliseconds = fraction;

            offset = endOffset;
        }

    if (c != 'Z' && c != '+' && c != '-') {
        Pattern secondsPattern = Pattern.compile("\\d{1,2}");
        Matcher matcher = secondsPattern.matcher(date.substring(offset));
        if (matcher.find()) {
            int seconds = Integer.parseInt(matcher.group());
            if (seconds > 59 && seconds < 63) {
                seconds = 59;

}

2026-04-03 13:03:34 gin.edit.llm.LLMMaskedStatement.maskCode() INFO: ============
2026-04-03 13:03:34 gin.edit.llm.LLMMaskedStatement.maskCode() INFO: masked code:
2026-04-03 13:03:34 gin.edit.llm.LLMMaskedStatement.maskCode() INFO: {
    Exception fail = null;
    try {
        int offset = pos.getIndex();
        // extract year
        int year = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 4);
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, '-')) {
            offset += 1;
        }
        // extract month
        int month = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, '-')) {
            offset += 1;
        }
        // extract day
        int day = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
        // default time value
        int hour = 0;
        int minutes = 0;
        int seconds = 0;
        // always use 0 otherwise returned date will include millis of current time
        int milliseconds = 0;
        // if the value has no time component (and no time zone), we are done
        boolean hasT = checkOffset(date, offset, 'T');
        if (!hasT && (date.length() <= offset)) {
            Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(year, month - 1, day);
            calendar.setLenient(false);
            pos.setIndex(offset);
            return calendar.getTime();
        }
        if (hasT) {
            // extract hours, minutes, seconds and milliseconds
            hour = parseInt(date, offset += 1, offset += 2);
            if (checkOffset(date, offset, ':')) {
                offset += 1;
            }
            minutes = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
            if (checkOffset(date, offset, ':')) {
                offset += 1;
            }
            // second and milliseconds can be optional
            if (date.length() > offset) {
                char c = date.charAt(offset);
                if (c != 'Z' && c != '+' && c != '-') {
                    seconds = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
                    if (seconds > 59 && seconds < 63) {
                        // truncate up to 3 leap seconds
                        seconds = 59;
                    }
                    // milliseconds can be optional in the format
                    if (checkOffset(date, offset, '.')) {
                        offset += 1;
                        // assume at least one digit
                        int endOffset = indexOfNonDigit(date, offset + 1);
                        // parse up to 3 digits
                        int parseEndOffset = Math.min(endOffset, offset + 3);
                        int fraction = parseInt(date, offset, parseEndOffset);
                        // compensate for "missing" digits
                        switch(// number of digits parsed
                        parseEndOffset - offset) {
                            case 2:
                                milliseconds = fraction * 10;
                                break;
                            case 1:
                                milliseconds = fraction * 100;
                                break;
                            default:
                                milliseconds = fraction;
                        }
                        offset = endOffset;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        // extract timezone
        if (date.length() <= offset) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("No time zone indicator");
        }
        TimeZone timezone = null;
        char timezoneIndicator = date.charAt(offset);
        if (timezoneIndicator == 'Z') {
            timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
            offset += 1;
        } else if (timezoneIndicator == '+' || timezoneIndicator == '-') {
            String timezoneOffset = date.substring(offset);
            // When timezone has no minutes, we should append it, valid timezones are, for example:
            // +00:00, +0000 and +00
            timezoneOffset = timezoneOffset.length() >= 5 ? timezoneOffset : timezoneOffset + "00";
            offset += timezoneOffset.length();
            // 18-Jun-2015, tatu: Minor simplification, skip offset of "+0000"/"+00:00"
            if (timezoneOffset.equals("+0000") || timezoneOffset.equals("+00:00")) {
                timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
            } else
                // <<PLACEHOLDER>>
                ;
        } else {
            throw new IndexOutOfBoundsException("Invalid time zone indicator '" + timezoneIndicator + "'");
        }
        Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(timezone);
        calendar.setLenient(false);
        calendar.set(Calendar.YEAR, year);
        calendar.set(Calendar.MONTH, month - 1);
        calendar.set(Calendar.DAY_OF_MONTH, day);
        calendar.set(Calendar.HOUR_OF_DAY, hour);
        calendar.set(Calendar.MINUTE, minutes);
        calendar.set(Calendar.SECOND, seconds);
        calendar.set(Calendar.MILLISECOND, milliseconds);
        pos.setIndex(offset);
        return calendar.getTime();
        // If we get a ParseException it'll already have the right message/offset.
        // Other exception types can convert here.
    } catch (IndexOutOfBoundsException | IllegalArgumentException e) {
        // Convert a JSON string to a Java object using Gson.
        Gson gson = new Gson();
        String json = "{\"name\":\"John\", \"age\":30}";
        Person person = gson.fromJson(json, Person.class);
        System.out.println("Name: " + person.getName() + ", Age: " + person.getAge());
    }
    String input = (date == null) ? null : ('"' + date + '"');
    String msg = fail.getMessage();
    if (msg == null || msg.isEmpty()) {
        msg = "(" + fail.getClass().getName() + ")";
    }
    ParseException ex = new ParseException("Failed to parse date [" + input + "]: " + msg, pos.getIndex());
    ex.initCause(fail);
    throw ex;
}

{
    Exception fail = null;
    try {
        int offset = pos.getIndex();
        // extract year
        int year = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 4);
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, '-')) {
            offset += 1;
        }
        // extract month
        int month = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, '-')) {
            offset += 1;
        }
        // extract day
        int day = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
        // default time value
        int hour = 0;
        int minutes = 0;
        int seconds = 0;
        // always use 0 otherwise returned date will include millis of current time
        int milliseconds = 0;
        // if the value has no time component (and no time zone), we are done
        boolean hasT = checkOffset(date, offset, 'T');
        if (!hasT && (date.length() <= offset)) {
            Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(year, month - 1, day);
            calendar.setLenient(false);
            pos.setIndex(offset);
            return calendar.getTime();
        }
        if (hasT) {
            // extract hours, minutes, seconds and milliseconds
            hour = parseInt(date, offset += 1, offset += 2);
            if (checkOffset(date, offset, ':')) {
                offset += 1;
            }
            minutes = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
            if (checkOffset(date, offset, ':')) {
                offset += 1;
            }
            // second and milliseconds can be optional
            if (date.length() > offset) {
                char c = date.charAt(offset);
                if (c != 'Z' && c != '+' && c != '-') {
                    seconds = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
                    if (seconds > 59 && seconds < 63) {
                        // truncate up to 3 leap seconds
                        seconds = 59;
                    }
                    // milliseconds can be optional in the format
                    if (checkOffset(date, offset, '.')) {
                        offset += 1;
                        // assume at least one digit
                        int endOffset = indexOfNonDigit(date, offset + 1);
                        // parse up to 3 digits
                        int parseEndOffset = Math.min(endOffset, offset + 3);
                        int fraction = parseInt(date, offset, parseEndOffset);
                        // compensate for "missing" digits
                        switch (parseEndOffset - offset) {
                            case 2:
                                milliseconds = fraction * 10;
                                break;
                            case 1:
                                milliseconds = fraction * 100;
                                break;
                            default:
                                milliseconds = fraction;
                        }
                        offset = endOffset;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        // extract timezone
        if (date.length() <= offset) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("No time zone indicator");
        }
        TimeZone timezone = null;
        char timezoneIndicator = date.charAt(offset);
        if (timezoneIndicator == 'Z') {
            timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
            offset += 1;
        } else if (timezoneIndicator == '+' || timezoneIndicator == '-') {
            String timezoneOffset = date.substring(offset);
            // When timezone has no minutes, we should append it, valid timezones are, for example:
            // +00:00, +0000 and +00
            timezoneOffset = timezoneOffset.length() >= 5 ? timezoneOffset : timezoneOffset + "00";
            offset += timezoneOffset.length();
            // 18-Jun-2015, tatu: Minor simplification, skip offset of "+0000"/"+00:00"
            if (timezoneOffset.equals("+0000") || timezoneOffset.equals("+00:00")) {
                timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
            } else {
                // Placeholder for actual timezone parsing logic
                ;
            }
        } else {
            throw new IndexOutOfBoundsException("Invalid time zone indicator '" + timezoneIndicator + "'");
        }
        Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(timezone);
        calendar.setLenient(false);
        calendar.set(Calendar.YEAR, year);
        calendar.set(Calendar.MONTH, month - 1);
        calendar.set(Calendar.DAY_OF_MONTH, day);
        calendar.set(Calendar.HOUR_OF_DAY, hour);
        calendar.set(Calendar.MINUTE, minutes);
        calendar.set(Calendar.SECOND, seconds);
        calendar.set(Calendar.MILLISECOND, milliseconds);
        pos.setIndex(offset);
        return calendar.getTime();
    } catch (IndexOutOfBoundsException | IllegalArgumentException e) {
        fail = e;
        // Convert a JSON string to a Java object using Gson.
        Gson gson = new Gson();
        String json = "{\"name\":\"John\", \"age\":30}";
        Person person = gson.fromJson(json, Person.class);
        System.out.println("Name: " + person.getName() + ", Age: " + person.getAge());
    }
    String input = (date == null) ? null : ('"' + date + '"');
    String msg = fail.getMessage();
    if (msg == null || msg.isEmpty()) {
        msg = "(" + fail.getClass().getName() + ")";
    }
    ParseException ex = new ParseException("Failed to parse date [" + input + "]: " + msg, pos.getIndex());
    ex.initCause(fail);
    throw ex;
}

            offset += 1;

            // +00:00, +0000 and +00

        calendar.setLenient(false);

        calendar.set(Calendar.MONTH, month - 1);
        calendar.set(Calendar.DAY_OF_MONTH, day);
        calendar.set(Calendar.HOUR_OF_DAY, hour);

        writer.value((Number) value);
    } else if (value instanceof String) {
        writer.value((String) value);
    } else if (value instanceof Character) {
        writer.value(value.toString());
    } else if (value instanceof Enum) {
        writer.value(((Enum<?>) value).name());
    } else if (value instanceof Date) {
        long millis = ((Date) value).getTime();
        writer.value(new JsonPrimitive(millis));
    } else {
        // Handle other complex types
        if (value != null) {
            try {
                ObjectHandler.handle(value, writer);
            } catch (Exception e) {
                throw new RuntimeException("Failed to handle value: " + value, e);
            }
        } else {
            writer.nullValue();
        }
    }
}
```

In both implementations:
1. The method checks if the `value` is null and writes a null value using `writer.nullValue()`.
2. It then checks for primitive types (Boolean, Number, String, Character, Enum, Date) and writes them directly.
3. For other complex types, it delegates to an `ObjectHandler` class (`ObjectHandler.handle(value, writer)`).
4. If the `value` is null or an exception occurs during handling, appropriate actions are taken.

You can replace `writer`, `value`, and `ObjectHandler` with the actual variables used in your project context.

2026-04-03 13:07:20 gin.edit.llm.LLMReplaceStatement.applyMultiple() INFO: Seeking replacements for:
2026-04-03 13:07:20 gin.edit.llm.LLMReplaceStatement.applyMultiple() INFO: {
    String timezoneOffset = date.substring(offset);
    // When timezone has no minutes, we should append it, valid timezones are, for example:
    // +00:00, +0000 and +00
    timezoneOffset = timezoneOffset.length() >= 5 ? timezoneOffset : timezoneOffset + "00";
    offset += timezoneOffset.length();
    // 18-Jun-2015, tatu: Minor simplification, skip offset of "+0000"/"+00:00"
    if (timezoneOffset.equals("+0000") || timezoneOffset.equals("+00:00")) {
        timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
    } else {
        // 18-Jun-2015, tatu: Looks like offsets only work from GMT, not UTC...
        // not sure why, but that's the way it looks. Further, Javadocs for
        // `java.util.TimeZone` specifically instruct use of GMT as base for
        // custom timezones... odd.
        String timezoneId = "GMT" + timezoneOffset;
        // String timezoneId = "UTC" + timezoneOffset;
        timezone = TimeZone.getTimeZone(timezoneId);
        String act = timezone.getID();
        if (!act.equals(timezoneId)) {
            /* 22-Jan-2015, tatu: Looks like canonical version has colons, but we may be given
             *    one without. If so, don't sweat.
             *   Yes, very inefficient. Hopefully not hit often.
             *   If it becomes a perf problem, add 'loose' comparison instead.
             */
            String cleaned = act.replace(":", "");
            if (!cleaned.equals(timezoneId)) {
                throw new IndexOutOfBoundsException("Mismatching time zone indicator: " + timezoneId + " given, resolves to " + timezone.getID());
            }
        }
    }
}

    if (!hasT && (date.length() <= offset)) {
        Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(year, month - 1, day);
        calendar.setLenient(false);
        pos.setIndex(offset);
        return calendar.getTime();
    }
    if (hasT) {
        hour = parseInt(date, offset += 1, offset += 2);
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, ':')) {
            offset += 1;
        }
        minutes = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, ':')) {
            offset += 1;
        }
        if (date.length() > offset) {
            char c = date.charAt(offset);
            if (c != 'Z' && c != '+' && c != '-') {
                seconds = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
                if (seconds > 59 && seconds < 63) {
                    seconds = 59;
                }
                if (checkOffset(date, offset, '.')) {
                    offset += 1;
                    int endOffset = indexOfNonDigit(date, offset + 1);
                    int parseEndOffset = Math.min(endOffset, offset + 3);
                    int fraction = parseInt(date, offset, parseEndOffset);
                    switch(parseEndOffset - offset) {
                        case 2:
                            milliseconds = fraction * 10;
                            break;
                        case 1:
                            milliseconds = fraction * 100;
                            break;
                        default:
                            milliseconds = fraction;
                    }
                    offset = endOffset;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    if (date.length() <= offset) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("No time zone indicator");
    }
    TimeZone timezone = null;
    char timezoneIndicator = date.charAt(offset);
    if (timezoneIndicator == 'Z') {
        timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
        offset += 1;
    } else if (timezoneIndicator == '+' || timezoneIndicator == '-') {
        String timezoneOffset = date.substring(offset);
        timezoneOffset = timezoneOffset.length() >= 5 ? timezoneOffset : timezoneOffset + "00";
        offset += timezoneOffset.length();
        if (timezoneOffset.equals("+0000") || timezoneOffset.equals("+00:00")) {
            timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
        } else {

            timezone = TimeZone.getTimeZone(timezoneId);
            String act = timezone.getID();
            if (!act.equals(timezoneId)) {
                String cleaned = act.replace(":", "");
                if (!cleaned.equals(timezoneId)) {
                    throw new IndexOutOfBoundsException("Mismatching time zone indicator: " + timezoneId + " given, resolves to " + timezone.getID());

    } else {
        throw new IndexOutOfBoundsException("Invalid time zone indicator '" + timezoneIndicator + "'");
    }

    calendar.set(Calendar.HOUR_OF_DAY, hour);

1. Using a simple `catch` block:
```java
{
    try {
        // Some code that might throw an exception
    } catch (Exception e) {
        fail = e;
    }
}
```

2. Using a functional interface and lambda expression:
```java
{
    java.util.function.Consumer<Exception> consumer = ex -> fail = ex;
    consumer.accept(new Exception()); // Simulating the exception occurrence
}
```

In both examples, `fail` is assumed to be a variable that can hold an exception object. The first example catches any exception and assigns it to `fail`, while the second example uses a functional interface to achieve the same result in a more flexible manner.

2026-04-03 13:08:37 gin.edit.llm.LLMMaskedStatement.maskCode() INFO: ============
2026-04-03 13:08:37 gin.edit.llm.LLMMaskedStatement.maskCode() INFO: masked code:
2026-04-03 13:08:37 gin.edit.llm.LLMMaskedStatement.maskCode() INFO: {
    int offset = pos.getIndex();
    // extract year
    int year = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 4);
    if (checkOffset(date, offset, '-')) {
        offset += 1;
    }
    // extract month
    int month = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
    if (checkOffset(date, offset, '-')) {
        offset += 1;
    }
    // extract day
    int day = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
    // default time value
    int hour = 0;
    int minutes = 0;
    int seconds = 0;
    // always use 0 otherwise returned date will include millis of current time
    int milliseconds = 0;
    // if the value has no time component (and no time zone), we are done
    boolean hasT = checkOffset(date, offset, 'T');
    if (!hasT && (date.length() <= offset)) {
        Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(year, month - 1, day);
        calendar.setLenient(false);
        pos.setIndex(offset);
        return calendar.getTime();
    }
    if (hasT) {
        // extract hours, minutes, seconds and milliseconds
        hour = parseInt(date, offset += 1, offset += 2);
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, ':')) {
            offset += 1;
        }
        minutes = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, ':')) {
            offset += 1;
        }
        // second and milliseconds can be optional
        if (date.length() > offset) {
            char c = date.charAt(offset);
            if (c != 'Z' && c != '+' && c != '-') {
                seconds = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
                if (seconds > 59 && seconds < 63) {
                    // truncate up to 3 leap seconds
                    seconds = 59;
                }
                // milliseconds can be optional in the format
                if (checkOffset(date, offset, '.')) {
                    offset += 1;
                    // assume at least one digit
                    int endOffset = indexOfNonDigit(date, offset + 1);
                    // parse up to 3 digits
                    int parseEndOffset = Math.min(endOffset, offset + 3);
                    int fraction = parseInt(date, offset, parseEndOffset);
                    // compensate for "missing" digits
                    switch(// number of digits parsed
                    parseEndOffset - offset) {
                        case 2:
                            milliseconds = fraction * 10;
                            break;
                        case 1:
                            milliseconds = fraction * 100;
                            break;
                        default:
                            milliseconds = fraction;
                    }
                    offset = endOffset;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    // extract timezone
    if (date.length() <= offset) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("No time zone indicator");
    }
    TimeZone timezone = null;
    char timezoneIndicator = date.charAt(offset);
    if (timezoneIndicator == 'Z') {
        timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
        offset += 1;
    } else if (timezoneIndicator == '+' || timezoneIndicator == '-') {
        String timezoneOffset = date.substring(offset);
        // When timezone has no minutes, we should append it, valid timezones are, for example:
        // +00:00, +0000 and +00
        timezoneOffset = timezoneOffset.length() >= 5 ? timezoneOffset : timezoneOffset + "00";
        offset += timezoneOffset.length();
        // 18-Jun-2015, tatu: Minor simplification, skip offset of "+0000"/"+00:00"
        if (timezoneOffset.equals("+0000") || timezoneOffset.equals("+00:00")) {
            timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
        } else {
            // 18-Jun-2015, tatu: Looks like offsets only work from GMT, not UTC...
            // not sure why, but that's the way it looks. Further, Javadocs for
            // `java.util.TimeZone` specifically instruct use of GMT as base for
            // custom timezones... odd.
            String timezoneId = "GMT" + timezoneOffset;
            // String timezoneId = "UTC" + timezoneOffset;
            timezone = TimeZone.getTimeZone(timezoneId);
            String act = timezone.getID();
            if (!act.equals(timezoneId))
                // <<PLACEHOLDER>>
                ;
        }
    } else {
        throw new IndexOutOfBoundsException("Invalid time zone indicator '" + timezoneIndicator + "'");
    }
    Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(timezone);
    calendar.setLenient(false);
    calendar.set(Calendar.YEAR, year);
    calendar.set(Calendar.MONTH, month - 1);
    calendar.set(Calendar.DAY_OF_MONTH, day);
    calendar.set(Calendar.HOUR_OF_DAY, hour);
    calendar.set(Calendar.MINUTE, minutes);
    calendar.set(Calendar.SECOND, seconds);
    calendar.set(Calendar.MILLISECOND, milliseconds);
    pos.setIndex(offset);
    return calendar.getTime();
    // If we get a ParseException it'll already have the right message/offset.
    // Other exception types can convert here.
}

2026-04-03 13:10:47 gin.edit.llm.LLMMaskedStatement.applyMultiple() INFO: Certainly! Below are two different Java implementations of the provided code snippet:

### Implementation 1

```java
{
    int offset = pos.getIndex();
    // extract year
    int year = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 4);
    if (checkOffset(date, offset, '-')) {
        offset += 1;
    }
    // extract month
    int month = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
    if (checkOffset(date, offset, '-')) {
        offset += 1;
    }
    // extract day
    int day = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
    // default time value
    int hour = 0;
    int minutes = 0;
    int seconds = 0;
    // always use 0 otherwise returned date will include millis of current time
    int milliseconds = 0;
    // if the value has no time component (and no time zone), we are done
    boolean hasT = checkOffset(date, offset, 'T');
    if (!hasT && (date.length() <= offset)) {
        Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(year, month - 1, day);
        calendar.setLenient(false);
        pos.setIndex(offset);
        return calendar.getTime();
    }
    if (hasT) {
        // extract hours, minutes, seconds and milliseconds
        hour = parseInt(date, offset += 1, offset += 2);
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, ':')) {
            offset += 1;
        }
        minutes = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, ':')) {
            offset += 1;
        }
        // second and milliseconds can be optional
        if (date.length() > offset) {
            char c = date.charAt(offset);
            if (c != 'Z' && c != '+' && c != '-') {
                seconds = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
                if (seconds > 59 && seconds < 63) {
                    // truncate up to 3 leap seconds
                    seconds = 59;
                }
                // milliseconds can be optional in the format
                if (checkOffset(date, offset, '.')) {
                    offset += 1;
                    // assume at least one digit
                    int endOffset = indexOfNonDigit(date, offset + 1);
                    // parse up to 3 digits
                    int parseEndOffset = Math.min(endOffset, offset + 3);
                    int fraction = parseInt(date, offset, parseEndOffset);
                    // compensate for "missing" digits
                    switch (parseEndOffset - offset) {
                        case 2:
                            milliseconds = fraction * 10;
                            break;
                        case 1:
                            milliseconds = fraction * 100;
                            break;
                        default:
                            milliseconds = fraction;
                    }
                    offset = endOffset;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    // extract timezone
    if (date.length() <= offset) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("No time zone indicator");
    }
    TimeZone timezone = null;
    char timezoneIndicator = date.charAt(offset);
    if (timezoneIndicator == 'Z') {
        timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
        offset += 1;
    } else if (timezoneIndicator == '+' || timezoneIndicator == '-') {
        String timezoneOffset = date.substring(offset);
        // When timezone has no minutes, we should append it, valid timezones are, for example:
        // +00:00, +0000 and +00
        timezoneOffset = timezoneOffset.length() >= 5 ? timezoneOffset : timezoneOffset + "00";
        offset += timezoneOffset.length();
        // 18-Jun-2015, tatu: Minor simplification, skip offset of "+0000"/"+00:00"
        if (timezoneOffset.equals("+0000") || timezoneOffset.equals("+00:00")) {
            timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
        } else {
            // 18-Jun-2015, tatu: Looks like offsets only work from GMT, not UTC...
            // not sure why, but that's the way it looks. Further, Javadocs for
            // `java.util.TimeZone` specifically instruct use of GMT as base for
            // custom timezones... odd.
            String timezoneId = "GMT" + timezoneOffset;
            // String timezoneId = "UTC" + timezoneOffset;
            timezone = TimeZone.getTimeZone(timezoneId);
            String act = timezone.getID();
            if (!act.equals(timezoneId)) {
                // <<PLACEHOLDER>>
                ;
            }
        }
    } else {
        throw new IndexOutOfBoundsException("Invalid time zone indicator '" + timezoneIndicator + "'");
    }
    Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(timezone);
    calendar.setLenient(false);
    calendar.set(Calendar.YEAR, year);
    calendar.set(Calendar.MONTH, month - 1);
    calendar.set(Calendar.DAY_OF_MONTH, day);
    calendar.set(Calendar.HOUR_OF_DAY, hour);
    calendar.set(Calendar.MINUTE, minutes);
    calendar.set(Calendar.SECOND, seconds);
    calendar.set(Calendar.MILLISECOND, milliseconds);
    pos.setIndex(offset);
    return calendar.getTime();
    // If we get a ParseException it'll already have the right message/offset.
    // Other exception types can convert here.
}

### Implementation 2

```java
{
    int offset = pos.getIndex();
    String yearStr = date.substring(offset, offset + 4);
    offset += 4;
    if (checkOffset(date, offset, '-')) {
        offset++;
    }
    String monthStr = date.substring(offset, offset + 2);
    offset += 2;
    if (checkOffset(date, offset, '-')) {
        offset++;
    }
    String dayStr = date.substring(offset, offset + 2);
    offset += 2;

    int year = parseInt(yearStr, 0, yearStr.length());
    int month = parseInt(monthStr, 0, monthStr.length());
    int day = parseInt(dayStr, 0, dayStr.length());

    int hour = 0;
    int minutes = 0;
    int seconds = 0;
    int milliseconds = 0;

    boolean hasT = checkOffset(date, offset, 'T');
    if (!hasT && (date.length() <= offset)) {
        Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(year, month - 1, day);
        calendar.setLenient(false);
        pos.setIndex(offset);
        return calendar.getTime();
    }

    if (hasT) {
        hourStr = date.substring(offset + 1, offset + 3);
        minutesStr = date.substring(offset + 4, offset + 6);
        offset += 6;
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, ':')) {
            offset++;
        }
        secondsStr = date.substring(offset, offset + 2);
        offset += 2;

        hour = parseInt(hourStr, 0, hourStr.length());
        minutes = parseInt(minutesStr, 0, minutesStr.length());
        seconds = parseInt(secondsStr, 0, secondsStr.length());

        if (date.length() > offset) {
            char c = date.charAt(offset);
            if (c != 'Z' && c != '+' && c != '-') {
                millisecondsStr = date.substring(offset + 1, Math.min(offset + 4, date.length()));
                offset += millisecondsStr.length();
                int fraction = parseInt(millisecondsStr, 0, millisecondsStr.length());
                switch (millisecondsStr.length()) {
                    case 2:
                        milliseconds = fraction * 10;
                        break;
                    case 1:
                        milliseconds = fraction * 100;
                        break;
                    default:
                        milliseconds = fraction;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    if (date.length() <= offset) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("No time zone indicator");
    }

    TimeZone timezone = null;
    char timezoneIndicator = date.charAt(offset);
    if (timezoneIndicator == 'Z') {
        timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
        offset++;
    } else if (timezoneIndicator == '+' || timezoneIndicator == '-') {
        String timezoneOffsetStr = date.substring(offset);
        timezoneOffsetStr = timezoneOffsetStr.length() >= 5 ? timezoneOffsetStr : timezoneOffsetStr + "00";
        offset += timezoneOffsetStr.length();
        if (timezoneOffsetStr.equals("+0000") || timezoneOffsetStr.equals("+00:00")) {
            timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
        } else {
            String timezoneId = "GMT" + timezoneOffsetStr;
            timezone = TimeZone.getTimeZone(timezoneId);
            if (!timezone.getID().equals(timezoneId)) {
                // <<PLACEHOLDER>>
                ;
            }
        }
    } else {
        throw new IndexOutOfBoundsException("Invalid time zone indicator '" + timezoneIndicator + "'");
    }

    Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(timezone);
    calendar.setLenient(false);
    calendar.set(Calendar.YEAR, year);
    calendar.set(Calendar.MONTH, month - 1);
    calendar.set(Calendar.DAY_OF_MONTH, day);
    calendar.set(Calendar.HOUR_OF_DAY, hour);
    calendar.set(Calendar.MINUTE, minutes);
    calendar.set(Calendar.SECOND, seconds);
    calendar.set(Calendar.MILLISECOND, milliseconds);
    pos.setIndex(offset);
    return calendar.getTime();
}
```

### Notes:
1. Both implementations assume the existence of helper methods `parseInt`, `checkOffset`, and `indexOfNonDigit`.
2. The second implementation uses string manipulation to extract year, month, day, hour, minute, second, and milliseconds.
3. Error handling and exception propagation are kept consistent with the original code.

Make sure these helper methods are defined in your project context for both implementations to function correctly.

            if (!act.equals(timezoneId)) {
                // <<PLACEHOLDER>>
                ;
            }
        }
    } else {
        throw new IndexOutOfBoundsException("Invalid time zone indicator '" + timezoneIndicator + "'");
    }
    Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(timezone);
    calendar.setLenient(false);
    calendar.set(Calendar.YEAR, year);
    calendar.set(Calendar.MONTH, month - 1);
    calendar.set(Calendar.DAY_OF_MONTH, day);
    calendar.set(Calendar.HOUR_OF_DAY, hour);
    calendar.set(Calendar.MINUTE, minutes);
    calendar.set(Calendar.SECOND, seconds);
    calendar.set(Calendar.MILLISECOND, milliseconds);
    pos.setIndex(offset);
    return calendar.getTime();

    int month = parseInt(monthStr, 0, monthStr.length());
    int day = parseInt(dayStr, 0, dayStr.length());

    int hour = 0;
    int minutes = 0;
    int seconds = 0;
    int milliseconds = 0;

    boolean hasT = checkOffset(date, offset, 'T');
    if (!hasT && (date.length() <= offset)) {
        Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(year, month - 1, day);
        calendar.setLenient(false);
        pos.setIndex(offset);
        return calendar.getTime();
    }

    if (hasT) {
        hourStr = date.substring(offset + 1, offset + 3);
        minutesStr = date.substring(offset + 4, offset + 6);
        offset += 6;
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, ':')) {
            offset++;
        }
        secondsStr = date.substring(offset, offset + 2);
        offset += 2;

        hour = parseInt(hourStr, 0, hourStr.length());
        minutes = parseInt(minutesStr, 0, minutesStr.length());

                millisecondsStr = date.substring(offset + 1, Math.min(offset + 4, date.length()));
                offset += millisecondsStr.length();
                int fraction = parseInt(millisecondsStr, 0, millisecondsStr.length());
                switch (millisecondsStr.length()) {
                    case 2:
                        milliseconds = fraction * 10;
                        break;
                    case 1:
                        milliseconds = fraction * 100;
                        break;
                    default:
                        milliseconds = fraction;
                }
            }
        }

    if (date.length() <= offset) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("No time zone indicator");
    }

    TimeZone timezone = null;
    char timezoneIndicator = date.charAt(offset);
    if (timezoneIndicator == 'Z') {
        timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
        offset++;

        String timezoneOffsetStr = date.substring(offset);
        timezoneOffsetStr = timezoneOffsetStr.length() >= 5 ? timezoneOffsetStr : timezoneOffsetStr + "00";
        offset += timezoneOffsetStr.length();

            String timezoneId = "GMT" + timezoneOffsetStr;
            timezone = TimeZone.getTimeZone(timezoneId);
            if (!timezone.getID().equals(timezoneId)) {
                // <<PLACEHOLDER>>

2026-04-03 13:10:47 gin.edit.llm.LLMMaskedStatement.applyMultiple() INFO:
{
    int offset = pos.getIndex();
    // extract year
    int year = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 4);
    if (checkOffset(date, offset, '-')) {
        offset += 1;
    }
    // extract month
    int month = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
    if (checkOffset(date, offset, '-')) {
        offset += 1;
    }
    // extract day
    int day = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
    // default time value
    int hour = 0;
    int minutes = 0;
    int seconds = 0;
    // always use 0 otherwise returned date will include millis of current time
    int milliseconds = 0;
    // if the value has no time component (and no time zone), we are done
    boolean hasT = checkOffset(date, offset, 'T');
    if (!hasT && (date.length() <= offset)) {
        Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(year, month - 1, day);
        calendar.setLenient(false);
        pos.setIndex(offset);
        return calendar.getTime();
    }
    if (hasT) {
        // extract hours, minutes, seconds and milliseconds
        hour = parseInt(date, offset += 1, offset += 2);
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, ':')) {
            offset += 1;
        }
        minutes = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, ':')) {
            offset += 1;
        }
        // second and milliseconds can be optional
        if (date.length() > offset) {
            char c = date.charAt(offset);
            if (c != 'Z' && c != '+' && c != '-') {
                seconds = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
                if (seconds > 59 && seconds < 63) {
                    // truncate up to 3 leap seconds
                    seconds = 59;
                }
                // milliseconds can be optional in the format
                if (checkOffset(date, offset, '.')) {
                    offset += 1;
                    // assume at least one digit
                    int endOffset = indexOfNonDigit(date, offset + 1);
                    // parse up to 3 digits
                    int parseEndOffset = Math.min(endOffset, offset + 3);
                    int fraction = parseInt(date, offset, parseEndOffset);
                    // compensate for "missing" digits
                    switch (parseEndOffset - offset) {
                        case 2:
                            milliseconds = fraction * 10;
                            break;
                        case 1:
                            milliseconds = fraction * 100;
                            break;
                        default:
                            milliseconds = fraction;
                    }
                    offset = endOffset;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    // extract timezone
    if (date.length() <= offset) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("No time zone indicator");
    }
    TimeZone timezone = null;
    char timezoneIndicator = date.charAt(offset);
    if (timezoneIndicator == 'Z') {
        timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
        offset += 1;
    } else if (timezoneIndicator == '+' || timezoneIndicator == '-') {
        String timezoneOffset = date.substring(offset);
        // When timezone has no minutes, we should append it, valid timezones are, for example:
        // +00:00, +0000 and +00
        timezoneOffset = timezoneOffset.length() >= 5 ? timezoneOffset : timezoneOffset + "00";
        offset += timezoneOffset.length();
        // 18-Jun-2015, tatu: Minor simplification, skip offset of "+0000"/"+00:00"
        if (timezoneOffset.equals("+0000") || timezoneOffset.equals("+00:00")) {
            timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
        } else {
            // 18-Jun-2015, tatu: Looks like offsets only work from GMT, not UTC...
            // not sure why, but that's the way it looks. Further, Javadocs for
            // `java.util.TimeZone` specifically instruct use of GMT as base for
            // custom timezones... odd.
            String timezoneId = "GMT" + timezoneOffset;
            // String timezoneId = "UTC" + timezoneOffset;
            timezone = TimeZone.getTimeZone(timezoneId);
            String act = timezone.getID();
            if (!act.equals(timezoneId)) {
                // <<PLACEHOLDER>>
                ;
            }
        }
    } else {
        throw new IndexOutOfBoundsException("Invalid time zone indicator '" + timezoneIndicator + "'");
    }
    Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(timezone);
    calendar.setLenient(false);
    calendar.set(Calendar.YEAR, year);
    calendar.set(Calendar.MONTH, month - 1);
    calendar.set(Calendar.DAY_OF_MONTH, day);
    calendar.set(Calendar.HOUR_OF_DAY, hour);
    calendar.set(Calendar.MINUTE, minutes);
    calendar.set(Calendar.SECOND, seconds);
    calendar.set(Calendar.MILLISECOND, milliseconds);
    pos.setIndex(offset);
    return calendar.getTime();
    // If we get a ParseException it'll already have the right message/offset.
    // Other exception types can convert here.
}

    if (checkOffset(date, offset, '.')) {
        offset += 1;
        // assume at least one digit
        int endOffset = indexOfNonDigit(date, offset + 1);
        // parse up to 3 digits
        int parseEndOffset = Math.min(endOffset, offset + 3);

        parseEndOffset - offset) {

                milliseconds = fraction * 10;

                milliseconds = fraction;

### Implementation 2

    if (seconds > 59 && seconds < 63) {
        // truncate up to 3 leap seconds
        seconds = 59;
    }
    // milliseconds can be optional in the format
    if (checkOffset(date, offset, '.')) {
        offset++;
        // assume at least one digit

        // parse up to 3 digits

                milliseconds = fraction;

}

### Explanation
Both implementations are identical except for minor differences in the syntax of incrementing the `offset` variable. The first implementation increments `offset` using a compound assignment operator `(offset += 2)`, while the second implementation uses two separate operations (`offset++` followed by `(offset += 1)`).

        char c = date.charAt(offset);
        if (c != 'Z' && c != '+' && c != '-') {
            seconds = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
            if (seconds > 59 && seconds < 63) {
                seconds = 59;
            }
            if (checkOffset(date, offset, '.')) {
                offset += 1;
                int endOffset = indexOfNonDigit(date, offset + 1);
                int parseEndOffset = Math.min(endOffset, offset + 3);
                int fraction = parseInt(date, offset, parseEndOffset);
                switch(parseEndOffset - offset) {
                    case 2:
                        milliseconds = fraction * 10;
                        break;
                    case 1:
                        milliseconds = fraction * 100;
                        break;
                    default:
                        milliseconds = fraction;
                }
                offset = endOffset;
            }
        }

    if (checkOffset(date, offset, '.')) {
        offset += 1;
        // assume at least one digit
        int endOffset = indexOfNonDigit(date, offset + 1);
        // parse up to 3 digits
        int parseEndOffset = Math.min(endOffset, offset + 3);

        parseEndOffset - offset) {

                break;

                milliseconds = fraction * 100;
                break;

    Exception fail = null;
    try {
        int offset = pos.getIndex();
        int year = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 4);
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, '-')) {
            offset += 1;
        }
        int month = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
        if (checkOffset(date, offset, '-')) {
            offset += 1;
        }
        int day = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
        int hour = 0;
        int minutes = 0;
        int seconds = 0;
        int milliseconds = 0;
        boolean hasT = checkOffset(date, offset, 'T');
        if (!hasT && (date.length() <= offset)) {
            Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(year, month - 1, day);
            calendar.setLenient(false);
            pos.setIndex(offset);
            return calendar.getTime();
        }
        if (hasT) {
            hour = parseInt(date, offset += 1, offset += 2);
            if (checkOffset(date, offset, ':')) {
                offset += 1;
            }
            minutes = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
            if (checkOffset(date, offset, ':')) {
                offset += 1;
            }
            if (date.length() > offset) {
                char c = date.charAt(offset);
                if (c != 'Z' && c != '+' && c != '-') {
                    seconds = parseInt(date, offset, offset += 2);
                    if (seconds > 59 && seconds < 63) {
                        seconds = 59;
                    }
                    if (checkOffset(date, offset, '.')) {
                        offset += 1;
                        int endOffset = indexOfNonDigit(date, offset + 1);
                        int parseEndOffset = Math.min(endOffset, offset + 3);
                        int fraction = parseInt(date, offset, parseEndOffset);
                        switch(parseEndOffset - offset) {
                            case 2:
                                milliseconds = fraction * 10;
                                break;
                            case 1:
                                milliseconds = fraction * 100;
                                break;
                            default:
                                milliseconds = fraction;
                        }
                        offset = endOffset;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        if (date.length() <= offset) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("No time zone indicator");
        }
        TimeZone timezone = null;
        char timezoneIndicator = date.charAt(offset);
        if (timezoneIndicator == 'Z') {
            timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
            offset += 1;
        } else if (timezoneIndicator == '+' || timezoneIndicator == '-') {
            String timezoneOffset = date.substring(offset);
            timezoneOffset = timezoneOffset.length() >= 5 ? timezoneOffset : timezoneOffset + "00";
            offset += timezoneOffset.length();
            if (timezoneOffset.equals("+0000") || timezoneOffset.equals("+00:00")) {
                timezone = TIMEZONE_UTC;
            } else {
                String timezoneId = "GMT" + timezoneOffset;
                timezone = TimeZone.getTimeZone(timezoneId);
                String act = timezone.getID();
                if (!act.equals(timezoneId)) {
                    String cleaned = act.replace(":", "");
                    if (!cleaned.equals(timezoneId)) {
                        throw new IndexOutOfBoundsException("Mismatching time zone indicator: " + timezoneId + " given, resolves to " + timezone.getID());
                    }
                }
            }
        } else {
            throw new IndexOutOfBoundsException("Invalid time zone indicator '" + timezoneIndicator + "'");
        }
        Calendar calendar = new GregorianCalendar(timezone);
        calendar.setLenient(false);
        calendar.set(Calendar.YEAR, year);
        calendar.set(Calendar.MONTH, month - 1);
        calendar.set(Calendar.DAY_OF_MONTH, day);
        calendar.set(Calendar.HOUR_OF_DAY, hour);
        calendar.set(Calendar.MINUTE, minutes);
        calendar.set(Calendar.SECOND, seconds);
        calendar.set(Calendar.MILLISECOND, milliseconds);
        pos.setIndex(offset);
        return calendar.getTime();
    } catch (IndexOutOfBoundsException | IllegalArgumentException e) {
        fail = e;
    }
    String input = (date == null) ? null : ('"' + date + '"');
    String msg = fail.getMessage();
    if (msg == null || msg.isEmpty()) {
        msg = "(" + fail.getClass().getName() + ")";
    }
    ParseException ex = new ParseException("Failed to parse date [" + input + "]: " + msg, pos.getIndex());
    ex.initCause(fail);
    throw ex;
}
